<user_name>Beth Maldonado<//user_name>< text>
Here's my very in depth review of DD. The first time my husband and I are here it was fairly new and unfortunately the sandwiches we got that day were not great. Neither of us were impressed. The bread was really dry and they were just very meh. However, I definitely like to give second chances and since the place was new I went back months later with my son. This time it was very good. Had a chef salad and my son a turkey sandwich. We both agreed we'd be back. I have been here three times since. The food is good. The service is ok. It's never blown my mind. Almost every time there's been a mistake of some sort. One worker also tried to sway me away from certain things I was thinking about ordering which I thought was weird.. and we've waited long times for our order when the store was very slow. I can forgive all these things because the food is tasty. There's one big problem  with this place though. One that will prevent us from eating here on a regular basis and that's the prices. They are ridiculously expensive. How in God's green earth does a sandwich combo and one medium sandwich with a cup of soup cost $36? Two meals at a sandwich shop cost me almost $40. I can't justify blowing that kind of money very often on a lunch place.</text>

<name>Daniel Lamas< /name><Date>1616386582093< /Date><rate>5< /rate>< text>
It was a very challenging and fun hike. There is more than enough room for parking, so if you know you're gonna challenge yourself, you can pretty much park next to the entrance of the trail. The hike is ALL uphill and the steep terrain can be very slippery and difficult to navigate. This hike is not easy by any means and nike shoes are definitely not recommended. Once at the top, you have spectacular views of the Burbank, Glendale, and Griffith park areas. This trail even leads up to Mount Thom so if you're feeling extra adventurous, check it out. I definitely recommend.<//text>

< Text>
The statue of Miss American Green Cross at its trailhead is a beautiful reminder of early American reforestation history. Sculpted by Frederick Willard Potter in 1928 as a symbol of conservation movement in the U. S. and particularly Glendale to save the forests of America.</Text>

[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN0VPiAI5o-H2ATc3MhK8sLX6tzDgSGKoA3CE7f=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics>
< Review>
hidden gem of a hike behind the suburbs of glendale! free parking near the library. i saw two trailheads, my friend and i took the "seven trees one." it is quite steep so beware. wear proper shoes, bring sunscreen, and water for sure! the path is dirt/gravel so can be slippery at times. the views of glendale/burbank are pretty neat! unfortunately, it was quite smoggy today. there are many forks in the road, with not too much signage. my friend and i ended up going higher up the mountain and traversed along the verdugo motorway and the brand motorway, until finally making it back to the parking lot (7 miles). more signs/maps would be helpful... we were scared we got lost a few times! there were not too many people on the trail, which was nice. also water fountains/restrooms would be great additions to the trails!<//Review>

<Review>We live about 5hours away. Unfortunately, because of our timing, we arrived past 10PM, when the lobby closes, at about 10:30PM. We did called same day to let them know we'd be late, and was told it'd be ok, and to ring the lobby doorbell. We had some issues contacting the hotel staff after hours; was not sure if the after-hours-doorbell was actually ringing when we pressed, and also calling the staff-phone wasn't working. After about 10minutes of pressing the doorbell, 5minutes later our phone call finally made it through, and we got checked in swiftly. So, my advice: try to arrive during lobby-open hours to avoid any issues.Our room was great. We intentionally chose this hotel for it's much lower rate compared to other sites and the great reviews we read through. Hotel is about a 10minute steady-walk to the peir; because we had a 4year old in tow, it took a little longer, and we took paths where there were traffic-light-controlled crosswalks. Otherwise, if it were just us adults, we could have arrived at the beachfront in just under 10min.Hotel is just across the way from the Pismo Beach 'Welcome' spot, for close-by access for photo-op.Room was fine - again, know what you're paying for. Bed and pillows were not horrible so as to keep me uncomfortable, or give me any body aches. As others mention, the hotel is next to a on/off ramp to the highway, but again, it didn't affect us. < Text>
Like many motels in Pismo this one appears to cater to persons that don't plan on spending a lot of time in their room. All of the furniture was old and outdated, the rooms were cramped, the bathroom had broken tiles on the floor. There was a fairly large refrigerator in there in case you bring your own food. The coffee maker was a single cup coffee maker and was very mediocre coffee. It's free, but there is a really good coffee shop not far that I would recommend if you want something better. I feel like overall for the price it wasn't quite worth it but it was at least just a short 7-minute walk to the beach and food. So really it just depends on what you're there for. Also, the walls are thin so ya know... You'll hear a lot of things at night. If possible try to get a second story room.</Text>

<pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNqE1AxDdIBWB6a4WmNAJasj5aiJaI5r51fhpt_=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMEmVsmghCRqpsUf4M17YZpzmGiVDPL-kZmNmJu=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO3iTlmfAcbPCkkbmgHx7BkXN5BG_Ntqd5h0s3y=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOIAnvGtdYAQ6zbtgfeKuFs6xZ7P5MGw6GJVTTD=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics><name>Jennifer Vreeke</name>< Text>
Hotel is very easy to find and in a great location. Just a few minute quaint walk to the sand, it lies blocks from Pomeroy and the Pier (great for avoiding crowded and frustrating parking situations). We booked the afternoon of check-in, and had no issues when arriving at the front desk. It was a bit late, so we were met with short conversation.

The room was surprisingly more upscale and clean than I originally gathered from other pictures and reviews. The bed was extremely comfortable and the pillows felt like clouds. The King Bed room had a mini fridge (useful with leftovers), and a nice Vizio TV. The bathroom amenities were clean and upscale.

Having lived in the area for many years previous to this visit, this is a place I will definitely be staying again. Can't beat that ocean air! We were also lucky enough to see some bioluminescent phytoplankton glowing in the sand and waves at night, which of course is awe inspiring!< /Text>

<rating>5</rating><text>After hearing how good Yama San is from a few different friends my wife and I decided to go give it a try last night.  We were NOT disappointed.  Having lived in Dos Vientos for so long and seeing restaurant after restaurant come and go, I'm really hoping this one sticks around.
Kelli had their Beef Bulgogi, which is a shredded and seasoned beef served with white rice. I had the Kalbi, which is thinly sliced ribs seasoned and served with white rice as well.  Both dishes came with various side dishes, 10 of them in all.  Some of them we liked a lot, a couple we did not, and a few we thought were good.  The great thing is they are served in small sample size amounts, and they come all you can eat.  If you especially enjoy a particular one you can get as much of it as you like.  I was a fan of the potato salad and the shredded sweet radish.
I haven't tried it yet, but they also serve fresh sushi, which I have heard is excellent as well.
Please support this great local place.  I‚Äôd like to see them stick around.</text>< pictures>

< Review>
I just got home from my first visit to Yama San. I was skeptical about the fusion of Korean and Japanese food, but they don't seem to have fusion dishes, just separate sections of the menu. I had dolsot bibimbap and was pleasantly surprised. It was very good. The banchan was pretty decent. We got kimchi, cucumber kimchi, pickled pearl onions, fish cakes, potato salad... And I think I'm missing something. It was definitely priced higher than most Korean restaurants ($60+ tip for two people), but I'd say that's the price of Korean food in Newbury Park, particularly in DV. Sorry, I would've taken a couple pics.</Review>

< review>
We like to stop by Denny's on El Camino Real on occasion. We try to stay away during busy times like Saturday and Sunday mornings. We like the nachos, burgers, omelets, and pancakes. When we can, we sit at the bar area or in the booths near the bar. The wait time is hit or miss, sometimes speedy and other times slow. The portion sizes are pretty large. Food prices are okay but not too cheap.<//review>

<time>1615774547661</time><Rating>3</Rating>< Review>
It's kind of hard for me to review this place because my first experience, which was in the late afternoon and arlier in the week and it was amazin.  I ordered a new dish on the menu called Mama D's pot roast.  That was as bold move on my part because I rarely will even order a meat dish from a restaurant, unless I happen to be at Alexanders Steak House or something equivalent to that. Ok, so, to my surprise it was perfect.  The carrots & celery were cooked perfect, just the right crunch still in them.  I'm not into soggy vegetables.  The meat was tender and lean.  Very good quality and cooked perfectly.   I was sold.  I kept talking about it for days, to whoever would listen.  Now FF to last night.  I sold my friend on the idea of going to Denny's to get this amazing Mama D's dish and I had such a bad experience.  They gave me something that slightly resembled what I had ordered earlier in the weak but it tasted horrible. It was salty and soggy and they gave me the wrong flavored milkshake and well, it just spiraled downward from there.  Granted it was midnight and they were probably ready to go home or something?  Anyways, I guess I will chop it up to inconsistent.  It's a gamble, but what isn't?< /Review>

< review>
This Denny's is on the El Camino Real and is same as any other Denny's. The staff is good and the place is mostly full. If you are planning for Friday and Saturday late night dinner or snack, keep in mind this place is packed with people. The other positive I see that this place is located near many other food joint and is not secluded. Parking space is not at all limited and this place is wheelchair accessible. Good for kids and adults. Remember you do have many options around this place if you are actually looking for something more elaborate. I like spending time here as it's close to my place. I've frequented many Denny's restaurants throughout the US, and this one is my new favorite.   The Service is Excellent, the Food is Excellent and the price is usually the same wherever you go (but still good).
